last_verified: 2026-05-22 (sixtieth session — **issue [#198](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/198), the end-to-end spine of Chat attachments for Jarvis (parent [#153](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/153)) — attach one image in Jarvis Core; IMPLEMENTED via `/tdd`, committed (`1aab18a`), migration APPLIED to AAA prod, [PR #206](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/206) OPEN against `main`, #198 NOT yet closed**) from TheLaunchPad. Built the first slice of parent #153: a user in Jarvis Core can attach **one image** (JPEG/PNG/GIF/WebP) to a message — Jarvis sees it, it renders as a thumbnail in the user's message bubble, survives a conversation reload, opens full-size, and is **replayed on every later turn** in the 30-message window; deleting the conversation wipes its attachments from the bucket. Built via `/tdd` in an isolated worktree (`.claude/worktrees/198-jarvis-chat-attachments`, branch `198-jarvis-chat-attachments`, cut from `main` at `a3d61f1`). **Three logic modules, test-first (16 unit tests):** `src/lib/jarvis/attachments/normalize.ts` (`validateAttachment` kind+size gate; `resizeImage` `sharp`-backed shrink to a ≤1568px long edge), `storage.ts` (owns the `{org}/{conversation}/{uuid}.{ext}` bucket path + upload / load / conversation-prefix delete), and `content-blocks.ts` (`buildClaudeMessages` maps the `JarvisMessage` history into the Anthropic message-params array, replaying every image via an injected resolver, degrading a message to text if its image can't be read). **Integration:** new private `jarvis-attachments` Supabase Storage bucket + Organization-scoped read policy (migration `migration-198-jarvis-attachments-bucket.sql`, **applied to AAA prod** this session via the Supabase MCP, recorded there as `jarvis_attachments_bucket`); `POST/GET /api/jarvis/attachments` (upload + signed URL, 6-test route test); `DELETE /api/jarvis/conversations/[id]` (prefix-sweep then row delete, `belongsToActiveOrganization` gained a `jarvis_conversations` resolver); chat-route wiring through `buildClaudeMessages` with an org-prefix guard on the resolver; attach UI across `JarvisInput` / `JarvisChat` / `JarvisMessage` — `JarvisChat` mints the conversation UUID **client-side** so an attachment uploads under the conversation prefix before the row exists. The attachment reference is stored **inline in `jarvis_conversations.messages` JSONB — no `jarvis_attachments` table**. Full suite **872 tests pass** (133 files, +22); `tsc` clean bar the pre-existing `sync-folder-incremental.test.ts` error; ESLint **0 problems** on all changed files. One feature commit `1aab18a` (17 files, +1384/−34) on branch `198-jarvis-chat-attachments`, pushed; **[PR #206](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/206)** opened against `main` with `Closes #198` — NOT yet merged, so #198 stays open and the worktree stands. Remaining #153 slices unbuilt: PDF attachments, multiple files, department routing, prompt caching. See [[2026-05-22-198-jarvis-chat-attachments]].

The new company is an ordinary contact — it appears in the Contacts tab and is editable there. **TDD ran as 13 red→green cycles** — 7 in `insurance-picker.test.ts` (guard across empty / exact-match / near-match / no-match; validator across valid / malformed / empty) and 6 new in `insurance-company-picker.test.tsx` (affordance appears with no exact match; withheld on an exact match; inline form expands prefilled and non-modal; submit creates a `role='insurance'` contact and auto-selects it; malformed email rejected with no insert; blank email allowed). last_verified: 2026-05-21 (fifty-seventh session — **issue [#187](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/187), the last slice of PRD [#45](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/45) (intake-form quality-of-life) — the migration flipping `when_happened` field-type `text` → `date` in existing orgs' saved `form_config`; IMPLEMENTED via `/tdd`, [PR #192](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/192) MERGED (`17713b5`), the migration APPLIED to AAA prod, and the live result browser-verified — PRD #45 fully delivered and CLOSED**) from Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local. Continued PRD #45 — built **#187, the companion migration to #184**: #184 updated only the intake-form builder *seed*, so orgs created before #184 still carry `when_happened` as field-type `"text"` in their stored `form_config.config` JSONB and would never get the new masked-date renderer; #187 flips that field's `type` to `"date"` in every existing `form_config` row that has it, leaving every other field and key untouched. Built via `/tdd` in an isolated worktree (`.claude/worktrees/187-form-config-migration`, branch `187-form-config-when-happened-date`, cut from `origin/main` at `04cce03`). Three SQL files in `supabase/`, mirroring the #186 three-file pattern: **`migration-187-form-config-when-happened-date.sql`** — the migration; a session-local `pg_temp.flip_when_happened_type(jsonb)` helper walks `config→sections→fields`, rewrites only the `when_happened` field's `type` to `"date"` and rebuilds both arrays in original order, driving both the pre-count and the `UPDATE` (rule written once, no permanent schema surface); idempotent (the `config IS DISTINCT FROM flip(config)` predicate skips rows already on `date` or with no `when_happened`, so `updated_at` is not bumped needlessly); a safety assertion aborts if the changed count drifts from the pre-count. **`migration-187-dry-run.sql`** — read-only would-change / already-date / no-`when_happened` counts + a `when_happened.type` breakdown. **`migration-187-smoke-test.sql`** — the TDD test artifact kept as a committed self-checking script (`begin; … rollback;`): a transform-parity battery (C1–C4) + the exact migration `UPDATE` exercised on a seeded temp table shaped like `form_config` (C5–C6). **TDD ran as 6 red→green cycles executed against the live AAA-prod DB via the Supabase MCP `execute_sql`** — temp tables / `pg_temp` functions only, no real rows touched (no local Postgres; scratch Supabase is paused); genuine RED shown for C1 (an identity-stub helper leaves `when_happened` on `text`) and C5 (an `UPDATE` without the `WHERE` predicate bumps all 3 seed rows). Dry-run on AAA prod: 110 `form_config` rows — 8 to flip (all `text`), 0 already `date`, 102 with no `when_happened` field (unaffected — the 8 are the full 7-section default seeds, the other 102 are customized 1–4-section configs). One feature commit `cd044f3` (3 files, +406) on branch `187-form-config-when-happened-date`, pushed; **[PR #192](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/192)** opened against `main` with `Closes #187`, then MERGED (merge commit `17713b5`) — #187 auto-closed. **The migration was then applied to AAA prod (`rzzprgidqbnqcdupmpfe`)** via Supabase `apply_migration` (name `migration_187_form_config_when_happened_date`) after the user's explicit plain-text "yes apply" (per `feedback_supabase_mcp_prod_migration_approval`); post-state verified — 8 rows now on `date`, 0 on `text`, only those 8 got a fresh `updated_at`, the 102 untouched. **PRD #45 status**: all of its slices — #183 (phone util), #184 (date field), #185 (phone rollout), #186 (phone backfill), #187 (this) — are now implemented; with #192 merged, **PRD #45 is fully delivered and CLOSED** — all five slices #183–#187 closed and merged, wrap-up comment posted on #45. The `187-form-config-migration` worktree + its local/remote branch were removed post-merge. **Browser-verified on AAA prod**: an existing org (AAA Disaster Recovery — `form_config` predates #184) now renders the masked `DateField` for "When Did It Happen?" — live masking (`12312020`→`12/31/2020`), calendar popover, and future-date rejection ("The date can't be in the future.") all confirmed in the live app, which retroactively covers the outstanding #184 component browser-check. No Xcode Cloud build (nothing under `ios/`); the #192 merge's Vercel deploy is a web no-op (SQL-only PR). See [[2026-05-21-187-form-config-migration]].

Continued PRD #45 — built **#186, the migration that backfills existing `contacts.phone` rows to canonical E.164**, via `/tdd` in an isolated worktree (`.claude/worktrees/186-backfill-phone-e164`, cut from `2ef3328`). Three SQL files in `supabase/`: **`migration-186-backfill-contacts-phone-e164.sql`** — the backfill; a session-local `pg_temp.normalize_us_phone_e164(text)` helper drives both the pre-count and the `UPDATE` (rule written once, no permanent schema surface — user choice via a plain-English `AskUserQuestion`, over a permanent `public` function that would duplicate `src/lib/phone.ts` and over an inline-twice expression); idempotent (already-canonical rows skipped via `phone IS DISTINCT FROM norm(phone)`, so `updated_at` is not bumped needlessly); a safety assertion aborts if the changed count drifts from the pre-count. **`migration-186-dry-run.sql`** — read-only would-change / already-canonical / unparseable counts + a no-PII digit-count breakdown of the unparseable rows. **`migration-186-smoke-test.sql`** — the TDD test artifact kept as a committed self-checking script (the `migration-140-smoke-test.sql` pattern): E.164 parity vs `normalizePhoneToE164()`'s test battery from `src/lib/phone.test.ts`, then the exact backfill `UPDATE` exercised on a seeded temp table (`begin; … rollback;`). Normalization mirrors `normalizePhoneToE164()` in `src/lib/phone.ts` (#183) exactly: strip non-digits → 10 digits ⇒ `+1XXXXXXXXXX` → 11 digits leading `1` ⇒ `+XXXXXXXXXXX` → else unparseable. **TDD ran as 6 red→green cycles executed against the live AAA-prod DB via the Supabase MCP `execute_sql`** — there is no local Postgres (no `psql`/`docker`/`supabase` CLI) and scratch Supabase is paused, so the loop used read-only `SELECT` harnesses + session-local temp tables/functions; **cycle 4 caught a real data-loss bug** — an unguarded `UPDATE` set unparseable values to `NULL` — fixed with a `norm() IS NOT NULL` guard. Worktree + its local and remote branch removed at session end. last_verified: 2026-05-21 (fifty-fifth session — **issue [#185](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/185), slice 4 of PRD [#45](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/45) (intake-form quality-of-life) — phone formatting rolled out app-wide; IMPLEMENTED via `/tdd` and MERGED via [PR #191](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/191) (`04cce03`); #185 CLOSED**) from Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local. The session continued PRD #45 — implement **#185 — apply the shared phone util everywhere a contact/adjuster phone is shown or edited** — in a new isolated worktree (`.claude/worktrees/185-phone-rollout`, branched from `origin/main` at `2ef3328`, `node_modules` symlinked) via `/tdd`. **TDD'd** a new **`phoneMatchesQuery(phone, query)`** in `src/lib/phone.ts` — 2 red→green cycles + 5 regression guards, **7 new Vitest tests** — which digit-normalizes both the stored number and the query (reusing the private `tenDigits` helper, dropping a leading `1`) and substring-matches, so an E.164-stored number matches whether the query is typed formatted, raw, or partially; an empty-digit query returns `false` so name searches do not false-match phones. **Wired** `formatPhoneNumber` across **8 display sites** (job-detail contact / HOA contact / adjuster card / adjuster-search results, contacts list, estimate customer block, estimate detail, settings users) and `formatPhoneNumber` + `normalizePhoneToE164` across **4 editors** (job-detail Edit Contact / Edit Insurance-HOA / Add Adjuster, contacts add/edit dialog) — format-as-you-type on `onChange`, format the loaded value on open, write E.164 on save; and swapped the contacts-page phone search clause to `phoneMatchesQuery`. **Editor save sites are best-effort, never block** (user `AskUserQuestion` choice): a valid number saves as E.164, a non-empty value that will not normalize is stored as typed (no data loss), empty stays `null` — blocking the save with a toast and silently writing `null` were both offered and rejected. One commit `ee38a14` on branch `185-phone-rollout`, 7 files +74/−21; **817** Vitest tests pass (126 files, +7); `tsc` clean bar the pre-existing `sync-folder-incremental.test.ts` error; ESLint **0 new problems** vs. baseline. Together these two changes complete the push-to-iPad-testable automation chain: every future push to `main` triggers an Xcode Cloud build (~10 min), the archive arrives at App Store Connect already export-compliant (plist key), and is auto-attached to the DISASTER MASTOURS internal group (workflow post-action) — testable in TestFlight in roughly 15 minutes total with zero manual ASC clicks. Two unrelated TestFlight-flow issues were discovered while doing #147: builds 175–187 had been silently stuck in "Missing Compliance" status (requiring per-build manual "Manage" clicks before testers could install — fixed by the plist key), and even compliance-cleared builds were not being auto-attached to DISASTER MASTOURS (only ~5 of ~188 historical builds were auto-attached via the group's "Build Distribution: Automatic for Xcode Builds" toggle, which is unreliable — fixed by the workflow post-action). These explained why the iPad's TestFlight had been correctly showing build `1.0 (146)` as the latest installable build despite 41 newer builds existing in App Store Connect. Diagnosis: `src/components/jarvis/JarvisChat.tsx` `createConversation` was inserting into `jarvis_conversations` without `organization_id`; the `tenant_isolation_jarvis_conversations` RLS policy (`migration-build49`) has a `WITH CHECK` requiring `organization_id IS NOT NULL AND organization_id = nookleus.active_organization_id()`. Until `migration-build57` dropped the transitional `transitional_allow_all_jarvis_conversations` policy in prod, the missing column was forgiven; with build57 applied, every brand-new conversation insert started getting rejected. Both handlers now derive the target user from `ctx.userId` (resolved by `withRequestContext`): `GET` drops the `userId` param and filters both its reads `.eq("user_id", ctx.userId)`; `PATCH { mark_all_read }` uses `ctx.userId`, not `body.user_id`; `PATCH { id }` scopes the update `.eq("id", id).eq("user_id", ctx.userId).select("id")` and returns **404** when nothing matched (a non-owned notification ≡ a missing one — the #98/#101 convention). The logged-in-only gate (`{ serviceClient: true }`) is unchanged — notifications are per-user, not role-gated; no permission key introduced. Issue [#97](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/97) — the **Active-Organization scoping guard module**, the first slice (a tracer bullet) of PRD [#95](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/95) security-triage of the ungated logged-in-only endpoints. **One source commit (`419b181`), no migration, no Vercel deploy** (auto-deploys on PR merge). **New module `src/lib/request-context/belongs-to-active-organization.ts`** — the tenant-scoping guard for Service-client routes: a User-client route gets tenant isolation free from row-level security, but the Service client bypasses RLS, so a Service-client route must do the cross-Organization check itself. `belongsToActiveOrganization(client, locator, activeOrgId): Promise<boolean>` answers one boolean question; `ResourceLocator` is a union of a **direct** `{ table, id }` (table carries `organization_id`) and a **`{ jobId }` shorthand**; indirect resolution runs through a per-table `OrgResolver` registry (`directColumn` / `throughForeignKey`, seeded with `jobs` direct + `job_activities` → `job_id` → `jobs`); a table absent from the registry **throws** (never a quiet pass), and a missing / cross-org / null-`activeOrgId` resource all return `false` so routes 404 (never 403). **New test `belongs-to-active-organization.test.ts`** — 12 tests in the `evaluate-permission-rule.test.ts` style, reusing the `request-context-fakes.ts` `fakeClient`: direct / `{ jobId }` / indirect locators × in-org / cross-org / missing, plus broken-chain, null-org, and unknown-table-throws. **Verification**: typecheck clean on the changed surface (only the pre-existing unrelated `sync-folder-incremental.test.ts` `TS2322` remains); lint clean on both new files; full suite **354 green / 55 files** (baseline 342/54 — +12 tests, +1 file). last_verified: 2026-05-16 (eighteenth session — **slice #79 Request Context tracer FULLY IMPLEMENTED; [PR #87](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/87) MERGED to `main` at `546a4b4`; issue #79 closed** from Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local. One source commit (`b40f657`, squashed into the #87 merge); no migrations; Vercel auto-deploys on merge. **What shipped**: built two new modules under `src/lib/request-context/` — (1) `evaluate-permission-rule`, the pure access-control policy (no I/O): given a rule + the caller's facts (role, granted permission keys) it returns allow/deny — `adminOnly` → admin role only, `permission` (single key or array) → admin OR holds a key, empty rule → logged-in only; (2) `withRequestContext`, the wrapper — resolves the user, the Active Organization from the `active_organization_id` JWT claim, membership role and all granted permission keys, defers the decision to `evaluate-permission-rule`, and on denial returns a standardized 401 `Not authenticated` / 403 `Permission denied` so the handler never runs; on success hands the handler a Request Context `{userId, orgId, role, supabase}`, adding the Service client only on `{serviceClient:true}`, Next.js route params passed through untouched. Converted all 6 `expenses` API routes to the wrapper and removed the inline `requireLogExpenses`: POST → `{permission:"log_expenses",serviceClient:true}` (keeps its own `user_profiles` lookup for `full_name`), PATCH/DELETE `[id]` → same rule (the submitter-or-admin ownership check stays as route business logic), the four `by-*`/`*-url` GETs → `{serviceClient:true}` logged-in-only. 37 new tests (17 pure + 8 wrapper + 12 converted-route); typecheck clean incl. Next 16's route validator; lint clean; full suite 218 green. **#80–#85 are now all unblocked** (each was blocked only by #79) and grabbable in parallel — #80 contracts+item-library, #81 invoices+estimates, #82 accounting+QuickBooks, #83 jobs+payments+payment-requests, #84 settings, #85 email+Jarvis+remaining; **#86** (delete the four old gates + publish the ungated-endpoint list) is still blocked by #80–#85. (4) Filed PRD **issue #78** (`ready-for-agent`) — modules `evaluate-permission-rule` (pure decision function) + `withRequestContext` (wrapper); all three test layers selected (pure / wrapper / converted routes). (5) Ran `/to-issues` — broke #78 into **8 slice issues**, all `ready-for-agent`: **#79** (HITL, no blockers) builds both modules + all three test suites + converts the `expenses` routes as the tracer; **#80–#85** (AFK, each blocked by #79) are conversion batches — #80 contracts+item-library, #81 invoices+estimates, #82 accounting+QuickBooks, #83 jobs+payments+payment-requests, #84 settings, #85 email+Jarvis+remaining; **#86** (AFK, blocked by #80–#85) deletes the four old gates and publishes the ungated-endpoint list. **What's next**: #79 is the only unblocked issue — implement it next; on merge #80–#85 become grabbable in parallel. last_verified: 2026-05-15 (fifteenth session — **exploratory/planning: contract-template permanent-delete design grilled to shared understanding and filed as PRD [issue #76](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/76), `ready-for-agent`. No source commits** from Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local. `main` HEAD unchanged at `4632045`. **What this session produced**: (1) brought `00-NOW.md` current — it had silently fallen four sessions behind (frontmatter still read "twelfth session — #66 drag-to-pan"); the fourteenth-session entry below was added covering #69 + #70 + PRD #65 fully delivered, and the thirteenth-session #69 entry was never separately stamped (it lives in [[2026-05-14-69-form-builder-safety-net-shipped]] and is rolled into the fourteenth entry). (2) Grilled (`/grill-me`) and filed (`/to-prd`) **issue #76 — "Permanently delete contract templates"**: a `⋯`-menu "Delete permanently" action that hard-removes a contract template and its uploaded PDF. **Four user-facing decisions locked by Eric**: (a) delete is **blocked only while a customer is mid-signing** — a template referenced by a `sent`/`viewed` contract is protected; every other case (including templates with a history of signed contracts) is deletable, because a signed contract is already its own stamped PDF; (b) unsent `draft` contracts **cascade-delete** with the template (confirm dialog discloses the count); (c) an already-`signed` contract's original signing link **still serves its stamped `signed_pdf_path`** after the template is gone (graceful degradation in `build-public-signing-view.ts`); (d) **one-step UI** — "Delete permanently" lives directly in the templates-list `⋯` menu with a confirmation popup, no archive-first two-step. **Technical shape in the PRD**: FK migration on `contracts.template_id` (drop `NOT NULL`, FK → `ON DELETE SET NULL`, so `Contract.template_id` type becomes `string | null`); a new `hard_delete_contract_template(p_template_id, p_org_id)` Postgres RPC (raise-if-blocked, delete drafts, delete template — authoritative re-check at delete time); a new `DELETE /api/settings/contract-templates/[id]/permanent` route (gated + org-scoped, best-effort storage cleanup of `pdf_storage_path`); a new advisory `GET …/[id]/usage` route feeding the confirm/block dialog its counts; graceful-degradation edits to `build-public-signing-view.ts` + `sign/[token]` + `in-person` routes. **Deep module**: `template-deletion-eligibility` — pure function, input the referencing contracts as `{id,status}`, output `{deletable, blockers, draftIds}`, build first via `/tdd`. **Tests** (Eric selected all four): the eligibility module, the RPC, the usage endpoint, the signing-view degradation. **Open threads from this session**: the FK migration is unwritten — per `feedback_supabase_mcp_prod_migration_approval.md` its SQL must be surfaced for a plain-text "yes apply" before `apply_migration`; the pre-existing soft-archive `DELETE /api/settings/contract-templates/[id]` (the "Archive" action) lacks both `requirePermission` and an org filter — the PRD explicitly leaves that as-is and notes tightening it as a separate follow-up. **What's next**: issue #76 is `ready-for-agent` and self-contained — an AFK agent or the next session can implement straight from it (suggested order: FK migration → eligibility module → RPC → routes → signing-view degradation → list UI). Per `feedback_pause_between_issues.md` it was filed but not started. Also still queued, untouched this session: **#58 umbrella** has #62 (Restore voided) + #63 (Permanently delete voided) `ready-for-agent`; the **#68 real-email demo** remains on Eric's plate. **Mechanical state**: branch `main`, HEAD `4632045`, no source commits, no migrations, no Vercel deploy; working tree carries only the `00-NOW.md` edit + this session's handoff file, plus gitignored `out/`. **Memories**: none saved this session. Pre-#67 the SELECT pulled only string columns by name so the bug was hidden. **Fix**: `String()`-coerce non-null `row[column]` in `merge-field-resolver.ts:160-167` before `applyOptionLabel`. **Two more bugs caught while in the same file**: (A) `fetchLatestFormConfig` in `merge-fields.ts:70-80` had no `organization_id` filter — sign page uses `createServiceClient()` (RLS-bypassed), so on multi-org installs it grabbed the global-max-version row (Test Company v103 instead of AAA v5). `buildMergeFieldValues` now fetches `jobs.organization_id` first and threads it through. **no storage surface** (slice #60's sidecar pattern means the canonical signed PDF is always clean — happy-path test positively asserts `storageDownloads.length === 0 && storageUploads.length === 0` even on a signed-then-voided contract). **RPC**: new `restore_contract(p_contract_id uuid, p_restored_by uuid)` mirrors build59's `void_contract` style — DECLARE v_org/v_job_id/v_signed_at/v_first_viewed_at/v_sent_at/v_target + RAISE-on-missing guard; 2026-05-13 (evening — **void/restore/permanently-delete PRD published** on Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local, third session of the day after the morning design+spec+#57-publish and the afternoon #57-implement. **Standalone design-only session — zero source commits; one artifact: GitHub issue [#58](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/issues/58) `Feature: void / restore / permanently delete contracts from the job view` with `ready-for-agent` label, published via `/to-prd` after a 9-question `/grill-me` session.** **The user-visible bug**: today's `…` menu in `src/components/contracts/contracts-section.tsx:69-75` registers a `mousedown` doc-listener to close the menu, but the menu panel only stops `onClick`, so `mousedown` on a menu item closes the menu before the click event lands — visible symptom is "tap Discard/Void, menu disappears, nothing happens." One-line fix during implementation (switch listener to `click`, or stop `onMouseDown` propagation). **The deeper redesign** (the actual reason for the grill) introduces a two-tier lifecycle: `alive → void → restore-or-permanently-delete`, with **drafts shortcut to one-click hard-delete** (no void tombstone for failed-send leftovers). **Nine grilled decisions**: (1) **hard-delete, not soft-delete** — `DELETE FROM contracts WHERE id = ?` with cascades to `contract_signers`+`contract_events` already in place from build-33 (`migration-build33-contracts.sql:54,77`); rejected `deleted_at` tombstone column per `no real customers yet`; (2) **signed-PDF watermark goes to a sidecar path** (`${signed_pdf_path}.voided.pdf` or sibling) so the canonical signed PDF is untouched on void and restore is trivially clean; today's `void/route.ts:69-92` overwrite-at-same-key bug becomes the fix; zero existing voided-signed prod rows so no backfill; (3) **restore target status derived from preserved timestamps** (`signed_at` → `signed`; else `first_viewed_at` → `viewed`; else `sent_at` → `sent`; else `draft`) — no new `voided_from_status` column; (4) **payment-block applied to void AND permanent-delete, NOT restore** — permanent-delete re-runs the check at delete time (covers void-before-payment / payment-after-void case); extract today's inline check (`void/route.ts:46-66`) to a shared `assertJobHasNoPayments(supabase, jobId)` helper; (5) **drafts get a one-click hard-delete shortcut** — menu on draft row says "Delete draft" not "Discard draft", single confirmation, direct DELETE, no void step; (6) **light confirmation on permanent-delete** ("Are you sure? This can't be undone." Cancel/Delete) — no type-the-title or admin gate; rationale: already 2 clicks deep, payment-block catches worst footgun, solo user with no real customers; (7) **all three actions silent** — no automatic emails to signer on void/restore/delete; `build-public-signing-view.ts:156,209` already returns HTTP 410 on voided contracts so link-going-dead is enough signal; (8) **both Restore + Permanently delete behind the `…` menu** on voided rows (remove the `{!isVoided && ...}` gate at line 404); (9) **no confirmation on Restore** — one click → toast. **Module sketch confirmed**: 3 routes (`POST void` modified, `POST restore` new, `DELETE` new with status-branching), 2 new RPCs (`restore_contract`, `delete_contract`), 1 new event type (`'restored'` added to `ContractEventType`), 3 deep extractions (`computeRestoreTargetStatus` pure, `assertJobHasNoPayments` shared, `writeVoidWatermarkSidecar` extracts the inline overwrite). **Test scope: option C (full coverage)** — pure unit tests for `computeRestoreTargetStatus` (4 branches + edge cases) + restore-route integration tests (draft/sent/viewed/signed targets, signed-PDF preservation, audit row insert, has_pending_contract recompute, 404/409/401) + delete-route integration tests (draft no-payment-check path, voided with-payment-check path, sidecar+canonical storage cleanup, has_pending_contract recompute, 409s on alive contracts, 404/401) + void-route sidecar-behavior tests (watermark lands on sidecar key, canonical untouched, plus existing scenarios continue passing). 2026-05-13 (afternoon — **finalize refactor IMPLEMENTED** on Vanessas-MacBook-Pro.local, second session of the day after the morning design+spec). **Single source commit `83b5312` `refactor(contracts): harden finalize — idempotency, error-checked flip, unified audit rows` landed on `main`; issue #57 closed.** Implemented via `/tdd` skill with vertical-slice cycles. Per the morning handoff's open question, **chose option (b)**: no build card — issue #57 + `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-13-finalize-signed-contract-refactor-design.md` are the durable record. **Three fixes (matching spec)**: (1) **idempotency early-return** — `finalizeSignedContract` reads `contracts.status` + `signed_pdf_path` from DB as its first action; if `status === 'signed'` returns `{ signedPdfPath: <existing>, wasAlreadyFinalized: true, notifications: emptyNotifications() }` immediately (no re-stamp, no re-flip, no emails); (2) **error-checked status flip** — closes the 15h-deferred silent-failure bug; the `contracts.update(...)` now captures `{ error }` and throws via `sealContract`, so emails never dispatch on a failed seal; (3) **unified audit-row metadata** — every intended recipient produces one `contract_events` row with `sent: {kind, signer_id?, provider, message_id}` / `failed: {kind, signer_id?, error}` / `skipped: {kind, signer_id?, skipped_reason}` (reason ∈ `settings_missing | no_internal_recipient | no_signer_email`); audit-write failures fall back to structured `console.error("[finalize] audit row write failed", {contractId, kind, signerId, originalOutcome, auditError})` per `project_no_real_customers_yet.md` (durable secondary fallback explicitly deferred). **Internal structure**: `finalizeSignedContract` is now a ~25-line orchestrator over two private helpers — `sealContract` (transactional, throws on any failure, returns `{ signedPdfPath, stampedPdfBytes }`) and `dispatchNotifications` (best-effort, never throws out, returns the structured outcomes block). Plus a `recordOutcome(supabase, contractId, outcome)` helper that translates each outcome into the unified row metadata. **New return shape**: `{ signedPdfPath, wasAlreadyFinalized, notifications: { summary: {sent, failed, skipped}, outcomes: Array<{recipient, signerId?, to, result}> } }`. **Callers updated** (`/api/sign/[token]/route.ts`, `/api/contracts/in-person/route.ts`): both capture `finalizeResult` and `console.warn` the summary when `summary.failed > 0 || summary.skipped > 0`; **HTTP response shape unchanged**. **Test file** `src/lib/contracts/finalize.test.ts` (new, 783 lines) with an in-file Supabase fake scoped to exactly what finalize touches (no general-purpose mock pulled in — chain-builder over `.from(...).select.eq.limit.maybeSingle`, `.update.eq`, `.insert`, plus `storage.from(...).download/upload`; tracks every insert/update/upload). External deps mocked at module level (`./stamp-pdf`, `./resolve-merge-values`, `./email-merge-fields`, `./email`). **Seven tests, all 6 spec scenarios + happy path**: idempotency-no-op / status-flip-error-throws / happy-path-return-shape / mixed-outcome-dispatch / settings-missing / no-internal-recipient-resolved / signer-with-empty-email. **Test infra gotchas surfaced**: `NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL` must be `vi.stubEnv`'d in `beforeAll` because `appUrl()` is called for the internal-email `contract_platform_url` merge value; `vi.clearAllMocks()` clears call history but **preserves implementations**, so a top-level `beforeEach` re-stamps the email-module mocks each test (defaults: `sendContractEmail → resend/msg-stub`, `resolveInternalRecipient → "internal@example.com"`). **TDD flow** ran vertical (RED→GREEN per cycle): idempotency → status-flip-error → happy-path return-shape (the big rewrite — extracted helpers, defined outcome types) → mixed/skipped/null scenarios passed on first run after the structural rewrite. Diverged from the spec's "step 8: write tests last" — TDD puts tests first by definition. **Test results**: 7/7 finalize tests pass; **27/27 full repo** (one pre-existing transform failure in `src/lib/mobile/use-capture-mode.test.ts` for missing `@testing-library/react` is **unrelated** to this work — predates this session). `tsc --noEmit` clean on all touched files; `eslint` clean on all touched files. **Mechanical state at session end**: branch `main` HEAD `83b5312`, **one commit ahead of `origin/main` `9fb246d` at handoff write-time** (this session's source commit is local — the user's `/handoff` arg `then commit +push+merge` means this handoff vault commit + the source commit get pushed as a single sequence after the diff is shown); working tree clean except gitignored `out/`; **no migrations** (`contract_events.metadata` is `jsonb`, no schema change); **no Vercel deploy yet** (auto-triggers on push; server-side fix only, no UI changes); **no TestFlight**. **GitHub state**: **issue #57 closed** with implementation summary comment pointing at commit `83b5312`. No PR opened (work landed on main directly, matching morning pattern). **Memories saved this session**: none — decisions live in the spec + this handoff. **Open threads (none are finalize regressions)**: durable secondary audit-write fallback filed for ~Build 67 (when `no_real_customers_yet` no longer holds); manual email-resend flow out-of-scope for #57 (audit log is today's recovery surface); `@testing-library/react` install whenever next session touches mobile tests (pre-existing); TestFlight push (Apple Dev Program enrolled, still deferred); portrait-lock Info.plist Xcode rebuild from `63bc89e`; Finding-B regression test (airplane-mode untested); 65b.1 follow-up list (~6 items); Step 5 Supabase email templates; AAA QB sandbox token (expired 2026-04-21); 67c2 reviewer F4-F8; 5xx redactor sweep across ~80 routes. **Next-session smoke surface**: the next contract signed in prod is the production smoke for this refactor — worth watching the first prod signing event in Vercel logs to confirm `notifications.summary` warn-log doesn't fire on the happy path and that the new audit-row metadata shape lands as expected. **Reusable pattern note**: the in-file Supabase fake at `finalize.test.ts:170-300` is the first of its kind in this repo (prior tests fake localStorage or exercise pure helpers); if a second test consumer needs a Supabase fake, lift this chain-builder pattern — premature extraction is its own anti-pattern. Grilled the design through six decisions: (1) **one function** (`finalizeSignedContract`), same callers, internal-only restructuring; (2) **refuse-to-run-twice idempotency** by reading `contracts.status` first and returning `wasAlreadyFinalized: true` on retry — "smart partial-retry recovery" explicitly cut, manual resend is a future flow; (3) **error-checked `contracts.update(...)`** so the silent status-flip failure deferred from 15h's reviewer findings gets fixed in the same change; (4) **internal split into two private helpers** (`sealContract` transactional + throws, `dispatchNotifications` best-effort + never throws out); (5) **audit-row shape: medium** — one `contract_events` row per intended recipient with unified outcome shape (`sent: {kind, signer_id?, provider, message_id}` / `failed: {kind, signer_id?, error}` / `skipped: {kind, signer_id?, skipped_reason}` where reason ∈ `settings_missing | no_internal_recipient | no_signer_email`), plus `console.error` to Vercel logs when `writeContractEvent` itself fails; durable secondary fallback (separate table or structured-logging pipeline) explicitly deferred per `project_no_real_customers_yet.md`; (6) **richer return shape** `{ signedPdfPath, wasAlreadyFinalized, notifications: { summary: {sent, failed, skipped}, outcomes: Array<{recipient, signerId?, to, result}> } }`; "already signed" returns normal result not exception. Spec lives at `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-13-finalize-signed-contract-refactor-design.md` with eight-step work order — **steps 1-2 (idempotency check + error-checked update) are load-bearing safety fixes that could ship as their own commit**. Read the iOS plugin source directly: `CameraPreviewPlugin.swift:92-93` divides incoming `x`/`y` by `UIScreen.main.scale` (asymmetric — width/height NOT divided), and `previewView` is added to `webView.superview` at iOS UIWindow coords (origin = screen top including status bar), while our `getBoundingClientRect` returned CSS coords offset below the status bar by Capacitor's `contentInset:'automatic'` — combined ~47pt drift explained both bugs. **The fix is a design pivot, not a coord patch**: `7f96090` rewrote the layout so the camera viewport is FULL-WIDTH and FLUSH to the screen top (iOS status bar overlays directly on the live preview), with only the BOTTOM corners rounded. Native rect math collapses to `x=0, y=0` + `height = cssHeight + safeAreaTop` — x/y=0 makes the plugin's scale-division a no-op, and the safe-area-top probe (transient CSS div with `height: env(safe-area-inset-top)`) extends the native rect upward to cover the status-bar area so the CSS-wrapper's bottom corner masks land exactly on the camera's hard bottom edge. 2026-05-11 (build 65c SHIPPED + MERGED on Vanessa's MacBook Pro + Eric's iPhone — **PR #52 merged to `main` via merge commit `5877bbe` at 2026-05-11 20:51:36 UTC**, branch `build-65c-upload-pipeline` deleted from origin. Session resolved the two open Findings from 2026-05-09 Test 2 evening, shipped the fix, verified end-to-end on real iPhone against AAA prod with **174/174 captures landed across three smoke tests (zero data loss)**, and ran Task 17 cleanup. **Finding B (queue-drain anomaly) — H1 confirmed via on-device sidecar audit**: 52 sidecars in session `dea218ba-...` all `upload_state: failed`, `retry_count: 4`, `last_error: "Load failed"` (WKWebView's generic offline fetch error), taken_at spanning **02:48:41 → 02:49:05 UTC** (the FIRST 52 captures of Test 2); 52 failed + 48 succeeded = 100 = Vanessa's badge claim accurate. **Failure mechanism**: airplane mode ON before capture started; captures 1-52 fired upload attempts via the `'65c-capture-written'` event listener (commit `3cf8d04`); each fetch returned "Load failed"; worker burned retry budget `[1s, 5s, 30s]` per capture → `MAX_RETRIES=3` exceeded → `failed`; by 02:49:06 `@capacitor/network`'s offline event silenced new attempts, captures 53-100 queued as `pending`; airplane OFF → drain → 48 pending uploaded; 52 `failed` stayed because worker doesn't auto-retry failed items. **Finding C surfaced as bycatch**: 87 sidecars across 8 sessions on Jadon's WTR-2026-0020 job all in `upload_state: 'unknown'` — pre-65c data; the worker's `eligible()` filter on `upload_state === 'pending'` made them silently invisible. **Fix shape = Option C** (pause/resume worker on network state): `UploadQueueWorker` now holds `isOnline = false` pessimistic default + `setOnline(online)` method; `drain()` early-returns when offline; `NetworkMonitor.start()` signature changed to `(online: boolean) => void` emitting both edges + initial getStatus; provider wires `network.start((online) => { worker.setOnline(online); if (online) worker.drain(); })`; standalone post-scanAll `worker.drain()` removed (now triggered by initial network edge). Forward-compatible — the in-pass Task 3 web fix wasn't time-pressured because the column default makes existing web uploads produce correct rows immediately. **Reviewer-driven amend in Task 5:** code-quality reviewer caught a `cachedKey` value-cache race where two concurrent first-call `encrypt()`s could each generate a key and clobber each other in iOS Keychain (any data encrypted with the losing key would be unrecoverable). Fix: cache the **promise**, not the resolved key — `keyPromise: Promise<CryptoKey> | null` + `loadOrGenerateKey()` returns the import-key result directly + `.catch` resets the cache for retry. Third vitest case `concurrent encrypt calls share a single key (no race)` locks this in. **One in-bundle scope-creep fix in Task 6:** `camera-view.tsx:151` had a `const sidecar: CaptureSidecar = { ... }` literal annotation that broke against the now-stricter `CaptureSidecar` type — removed the explicit annotation (1-character fix; lets TS infer the literal as `WritableSidecar`-compatible). **Beneficial deviations from plan-snippets:** Task 3 + Task 10 use `.maybeSingle()` instead of `.single()` for `user_profiles.full_name` lookup (matches existing pattern in `src/lib/auth-context.tsx:62-66` and aligns with spec's stated defensive-fallback intent — `.single()` would throw on missing profile and break the upload, defeating the spec). Task 1's first vitest-config attempt over-engineered with `@vitejs/plugin-react`, `resolve.alias`, and dropped `include`/`exclude` — caught at controller-level diff inspection, amended to match plan byte-for-byte (no `.tsx` tests in the plan; alias unneeded for colocated tests). Task 10 implementer caught a missing `@capacitor/app` dep (not in plan) and `npm install`ed it (`@capacitor/app@8.1.0`); also added `if (!user || !orgId) return` guard so the worker never constructs with a null org (because `getActiveOrganizationId` returns `string | null`). **Test suite at session end:** 3 files / 12 tests passing — `crypto-vault` (3: roundtrip + IV-randomness + concurrent-no-race), `exif-read` (2: known fixture + non-JPEG fallback), `upload-queue` (7: 4 backoff-math + 3 stale-claim-recovery). **Mechanical state:** local `main` HEAD `9afbc55` (Task 0 docs commit, **1 commit ahead of `origin/main` at `2259dfe`** — not pushed); local `build-65c-upload-pipeline` HEAD `22f9297`, **never pushed to origin** (no `origin/build-65c-upload-pipeline` ref exists). `build-65c-upload-pipeline` was branched off `9afbc55` (so pushing the feature branch will also force-include the Task 0 docs commit). Header buttons (Camera ←, Save & exit) misfired only when the grid scrolled, matching a known WebKit issue where hit-test bounds for `position: absolute` children of `overflow: auto` containers desync from the scroll offset and route taps to whichever absolute element overlaps the *unscrolled* bounds — even when the user taps an element entirely outside the scroll container. Trade-off: swipe-to-delete removed from review tiles; Select + batch Delete in the footer and the Delete button in the expanded photo view both preserved. **Live iPhone smoke results** (Eric's iPhone, AAA prod, signed in as Eric's normal user): rapid mode 20 captures ✅ count reached 20; tag-after mode 5 captures ✅ all 5 saved with caption + tag; review screen renders 25 thumbnails ✅; tap-to-expand individual photo ✅ after `fc4e508`; header back-to-camera ✅ after `fc4e508`; Save & exit ✅ after `fc4e508`. **Tests deferred** to next iPhone session: Test 4 (file count via Xcode device-files browser — heavier than smoke warrants; 65c will exercise this surface implicitly via upload telemetry), Test 5 (100-rapid battery drain ≤5%), Test 6 (permission-denied recovery flow). **Save & exit lands on the job page but photos do NOT appear in the job's photo set — EXPECTED gap, not a bug:** plan §5.3 explicitly scopes upload-to-Supabase to **65c** (aggressive background upload + sync indicator UI + auto-delete after sync); photos save to `pending-uploads/{job_id}/{capture_session_id}/...` on the iPhone but have no pipeline to flow to the `photos` table. **65c is now THE gated next priority with the strongest possible justification: real-device smoke confirmed the capture flow works.** **Four 65b-followup UX gaps filed** (none are 65b regressions): (1) tag-after panel doesn't show preview thumbnail of the just-taken photo (crew need to see what they're tagging); (2) <3-photo grid layout looks lopsided due to the always-3-column layout (cosmetic; consider `place-content: start` + auto-fit columns); (3) swipe-to-delete regressed in `fc4e508` — restorable by structuring the tile so the swipe-translating element is a child of the in-flow click target, not the click target itself; (4) Xcode build console noise (UIScene lifecycle deprecation, Auto Layout grumbles about `_UIButtonBarButton` system toolbars, single `WEBP makeImagePlus err=-50`, `RTIInputSystemClient` keyboard chatter, "variant selector cell index" emoji subsystem output) flagged for a future native iOS hygiene sweep — all Apple-internal/harmless for now. **Two third-party / WebKit footguns documented for future sessions:** (a) `@capacitor-community/camera-preview` v8 leaks a `UITapGestureRecognizer` on the WKWebView in the `toBack: true` path — `stop()` removes the preview view (`previewView.removeFromSuperview()`) but never the gesture (confirmed by reading `node_modules/@capacitor-community/camera-preview/ios/Sources/CameraPreviewPlugin/CameraPreviewPlugin.swift:138`); mitigation defensive `CameraPreview.stop()` on any post-camera screen + avoid pointer-event-heavy interactive elements after camera has run in the same app session; worth an upstream PR (~3-line patch: track recognizer in `start`, remove in `stop`); (b) WKWebView hit-test bounds for `position: absolute` children of scrollable containers desync from scroll offset — prefer in-flow tap targets when the container scrolls. **Memory `project_no_real_customers_yet.md` saved** — Nookleus prod has no live external customers as of 2026-05-08; production data loss is not a risk factor when planning tests/migrations; default to "test against prod, sign in as your normal user" instead of scratch-Supabase rituals; will need to update or replace once external customers exist. **Push-to-main classifier guardrail** blocked direct pushes three times this session; Eric authorized each via the `! git push origin main` slash-command escape hatch. Could add a `.claude/settings.json` permission rule (`Bash(git push origin main)` or broader `Bash(git push:*)`) to streamline if iteration cadence demands; not added preemptively because the friction is intentional. **`build-65b-session-a` branch** is now at `0c7f7eb` on origin (1 commit ahead of pre-session `6362edd`); fully merged to `main` via PR #51; safe to delete but not done this session. `main` HEAD `fc4e508` in sync with `origin/main`, working tree clean (only gitignored `out/`), no migrations applied, four functional commits + one PR-merge commit on top of `c17e592` (the prior session's vault commit). No implementation this session — fresh session needed to execute the 11 tasks. **Scope: customer + internal post-sign confirmation emails with the signed PDF attached, on both `POST /api/sign/[token]` (remote emailed-link flow) and `POST /api/contracts/in-person` (iPad in-person flow), via a new shared `finalizeSignedContract` helper at `src/lib/contracts/finalize.ts` that owns stamp + upload + status flip + email dispatch + audit rows.** Helper extraction collapses ~60 lines of duplicated stamp pipeline currently inlined in both routes into a single call site; adds ~80 lines of email dispatch (one customer email per signer with `signer_id` audit metadata + provider/message_id on success; one internal email to `resolveInternalRecipient`; best-effort with per-email try/catch isolation so one bad signer email never blocks the others). Eric questioned legality. Determined: editing a signed legal artifact is content modification under ESIGN/UETA; safe path for a bad PDF is **void + re-sign** (matches DocuSign / HelloSign). Orphan `regenerate-pdf/route.ts` deleted with no replacement. An earlier intermediate brainstorm decision ("fresh re-resolve of merge values on regenerate") was identified as carrying its own legal risk (a corrected job typo would silently change the saved signed PDF) and is moot now. Lesson preserved: never re-derive signed-contract content from current state; treat signed PDFs as immutable. Other decisions locked: in-person flow sends same emails as remote (industry standard), every signer gets their own customer-confirmation email (homeowner+spouse pattern, not just primary signer), internal email goes to reply-to fallback (`eric@aaacontracting.com` for AAA's Resend setup), best-effort emails so signing always succeeds even on email failure, audit on success captures `provider` + `message_id` (symmetrizes with 15e's failure-only audit shape), shared helper not duplicated code. Plan structure: T1 pre-flight DB check (verify `contract_email_settings.signed_confirmation_*_template` cols populated for AAA + Test Co), T2 helper file alone (commit; no callers yet), T3 wire both routes (commit + push; deploys live), T4 deploy verification, T5–T7 three live smoke tests against AAA prod (remote / in-person / failure-path with corrupted signer-2 email and audit-row checks via Supabase MCP), T8 test-data cleanup with `SET LOCAL storage.allow_delete_query='true'` admin escape, T9 orphan deletion (separate commit so reversible), T10 postinstall + `/public/` worker cleanup, T11 final tsc/build/push + handoff. Subagent-driven execution recommended for the 11 tasks. `main` HEAD `c0b4011` 2 commits ahead of `origin/main` at session end (spec `71f6aed` + plan `c0b4011`); session-start pulled `0c3f16e..14edb05` from origin (PR #49 zoom controls on PDF template editor merged earlier today by Eric, separate from 15h). [[contracts-builder]] **Slice #70 (auto-fill checkboxes) SHIPPED to branch `claude/70-autofill-checkboxes` 2026-05-14 (fourteenth session). [PR #75](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/75) OPEN against `main` awaiting Eric's merge.** Two source commits: `ae6affb` `contracts: auto-fill checkboxes bound to intake merge fields (#70)` + smoke-driven fix `d1cd5f5` `contracts: auto-fill evaluator must use raw merge values not labels (#70 smoke fix)`. **What shipped**: a checkbox overlay can be configured as either "Customer ticks at signing" (today's behavior) or "Auto-fill from intake data" — auto-fill checkboxes bind to a merge slug (from the #67 registry) plus a list of match values, and at contract draft creation each is ticked iff the job's resolved value is in `matchValues`. Auto-filled checkboxes are non-interactive (disabled) at signing and customers can't toggle them. New pure `auto-checkbox-evaluator.ts` module (12 truth-table tests); two new validator error codes (`unknown_autofill_merge_field`, `empty_autofill_match_values`) with 6 tests; new `GET /api/contracts/preflight?jobId=&templateId=` returning the list of auto-bound checkboxes whose source slug resolves to null so `send-contract-modal` warns before send. Both `POST /api/contracts/send` and `POST /api/contracts/in-person/start` fetch overlay_fields, compute `evaluateAutoCheckboxes(overlay_fields, buildMergeFieldRawValues(...))`, and patch `contracts.customer_inputs` post-RPC (the existing `create_contract_with_signers` RPC has no customer_inputs param — patch separately, no migration). `PublicSigningView` gained `customer_inputs`; signer view filters auto-bound checkboxes out of the interactive overlay and renders them as `<input disabled checked>`. `requiredMissing` (client) and the server `missing` checks both defensively skip auto-fill checkboxes. Inspector grew a "Checkbox type" radio toggle in `field-inspector.tsx` with `CheckboxInspectorBody` + `AutoFillBindingEditor` — pill-typed merge fields show option labels next to raw values; storing happens on raw option values; an amber inline warning flags `matchValues` entries that aren't in the bound field's option set (non-blocking per spec). Auto-fill checkboxes get an auto-generated `inputKey` (e.g. `auto_a3f9b1cd`) so `customer_inputs` + the existing `stampPdf` path keep working with zero changes — the inputKey field is hidden in the UI per spec. **Mid-smoke bug + fix**: the first send attempt produced `customer_inputs.auto_residential_70 = false` even though `property_type=single_family` matched the binding. Root cause: `resolveMergeFieldValues` applies `applyOptionLabel` to pill-typed fields by default, so `buildMergeFieldValues` returned `"Single Family"` (label) while `matchValues` stores `"single_family"` (raw value). Equality match never fired. Fix: added `opts.rawValues` flag to `resolveMergeFieldValues` that skips `applyOptionLabel` + `LEGACY_TITLECASE_COLUMNS` title-case; new `buildMergeFieldRawValues` wrapper sets it; the three call sites (send / in-person start / preflight) switched to the raw variant. Labeled values were never correct for equality-match evaluation — they're only for display/stamping. Plus a regression test in `auto-checkbox-evaluator.test.ts` (`"matches against raw option values, not display labels"`) that pins this contract with both cases. **All 11 spec ACs PASS** end-to-end against AAA prod via the Vercel PR preview on Untitled Template (6) `ec9b8c74…` and job WTR-2026-0016 `27de9daa…` (Eric Daniels, property_type=single_family). DOM probe confirmed AC6/AC7: auto-fill checkbox `{aria:"Auto-filled checkbox", disabled:true, checked:true}`, customer-ticks checkbox `{disabled:false, checked:false}`. **Bonus smoke**: end-to-end sign + stamped-PDF visual proof — POSTed `/api/sign/[token]` with a 1×1 PNG, contract flipped `sent → signed`, `customer_inputs` merged to `{auto_residential_70: true, agreed_terms_70: true}`, opened the stamped PDF inline via `URL.createObjectURL` + `<embed>` — both X glyphs visible at (100, 700) and (200, 700) on page 1. Tests: **156/156 green** (138 baseline + 18 new across 2 files); `tsc --noEmit` clean on changed surface; preexisting `sync-folder-incremental.test.ts:246` error from #64 work remains. Smoke results posted as two [PR #75 comments](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/75#issuecomment-4454659558). No migrations applied (JSONB-only schema extension on `OverlayField`). **Smoke fixtures left on Untitled Template (6)**: two test checkboxes at PDF coords (100, 700) and (200, 700) on page 1 — `auto_residential_70` (auto-fill, bound to property_type ∈ {single_family, multi_family, condo}) + `agreed_terms_70` (customer-ticks "I agree to the terms"). Useful for future smoke runs; Eric can delete via the inspector. **PRD #65 contracts-template-builder is fully delivered pending PR #75 merge** — slices #66 (drag-to-pan), #67 (dynamic merge fields), #68 (email pickers), #69 (form-builder safety net), and #70 (auto-fill checkboxes) all shipped. **Per `feedback_pause_between_issues.md`: pause for review/approval before any next initiative.** Next session resumption point: confirm Eric merged + Vercel auto-deploys + #70 auto-closes. **New this session**: `buildMergeFieldRawValues` vs `buildMergeFieldValues` is the load-bearing split — raw for equality-matching against `matchValues`, labeled for display/stamping; the regression test pins this contract directly. **Open threads carried**: #69 follow-up `unknownMatches` warning is informational-only; #68 real-email demo still on Eric; cross-org caution if `buildMergeFieldValues` called with non-existent jobId; preview-route `SAMPLE_MERGE_VALUES` still on legacy field names. [[contracts-builder]] **Slice #69 (form-builder safety net) SHIPPED to `main` at `26e49f6` 2026-05-14 (thirteenth session). [PR #74](https://github.com/ericdaniels22/Nookleus/pull/74) merged, issue #69 auto-closed.** Three protections against silent breakage of contract/email templates when an intake field is renamed/redirected/deleted: (1) `TemplateReferenceLookup` module (`src/lib/contracts/template-reference-lookup.ts`) with pure `extractReferencedSlugs(overlay_fields)` + `buildReferenceIndex(templates, slugs)` (9 unit tests) and RLS-scoped `findReferencingTemplates(supabase, slugs)` returning `{ slug: [{ id, name, is_active }] }`; (2) server-side delete guard via `form-config-removal-guard.ts` (6 unit tests) wired into both `POST /api/settings/intake-form` and `POST /api/settings/intake-form/restore` — diffs prior vs new config, returns 409 with structured `blocked` array when a removed field's slug is referenced; (3) new `GET /api/settings/intake-form/usage` endpoint returning the same map for every slug derived from the active org's latest form_config. Form-builder UI: Inspector shows Field ID read-only with lock-icon tooltip (input value is `merge_field_slug ?? id`, the slug authors see in `{{...}}` tokens); blue "Used by N" badge on each canvas field row with stopPropagation-gated click that expands an inline list of referencing templates; `maps_to` change on a referenced field triggers a confirm modal listing templates with Cancel/Change-anyway; delete is blocked client-side with a modal listing templates + a "Hide instead" CTA that flips `visible:false`; 409 responses are surfaced as toast + reload as defense-in-depth against races. **AC6 forced a corrective change to `buildMergeFieldRegistry`** — from "skip hidden" to "include hidden, mark `hidden: true`" — so existing contracts continue resolving from `job_custom_fields` after a field is hidden; picker consumers (`field-inspector`, `email-template-field`, `payment-email-template-field`) and `template-pdf-editor`'s default pick now filter `r.hidden` so authors can't pick hidden fields for new chips. Two registry-test cases updated to reflect the new "kept-with-hidden" semantics. Six-AC smoke run against AAA prod via the Vercel PR preview, all PASS, results posted as a PR comment before merge. No migrations applied (pure application-layer feature). [[build-15h-followup]] **Chrome `/sign/[token]` hang — email-iframe sandbox inheritance fix — SHIPPED 2026-05-08.** Closes finding #4 (final 15h-deferred UX item) — Chrome rendering `/sign/[token]` as a stuck "Loading PDF…" shell while Safari rendered fine. Single-commit fix `d9f92ef` on `main`, pushed to `origin/main`. One-line edit at `src/components/email-reader.tsx:62`: `sandbox="allow-same-origin allow-popups"` → `sandbox="allow-same-origin allow-popups allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox"`. **Root cause:** the in-app `/email` inbox renders email body HTML inside `<iframe sandbox="allow-same-origin allow-popups">` with `<base target="_blank">` injected so every link opens a new tab. Per HTML spec, popups opened from a sandboxed iframe inherit the parent's sandbox flag set unless `allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox` is also granted; inheritance carried `allow-scripts`'s absence into the new tab → React/Next/pdfjs scripts blocked at parse time → SSR shell rendered (header + "Loading PDF…" + footer) but never hydrated → no PDF fetch ever attempted. Console signature: 28× "Blocked script execution because document's frame is sandboxed and the 'allow-scripts' permission is not set." Same exact error signature 15e fixed for a different cause (pdf.js fake-worker fallback iframe was sandboxed); this time the parent tab itself was sandboxed via inheritance — the cause was upstream. **Diagnosis was the work; the fix was one token.** Three-context repro nailed it: incognito-paste rendered, MCP-controlled tab in same regular Chrome profile rendered (`navigator.serviceWorker.getRegistrations() = []`, `caches.keys() = []`, `pdfjs.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc = "/_next/static/media/pdf.worker.min.0wghn0~9oxou6.mjs"`, zero console errors), but click-from-email in regular Chrome still hung — differentiator was the navigation path, not the URL or the cache or login state. Eric's initial hypothesis ("logged in on Chrome but not on Safari?") was checked and ruled out via four-bullet falsification: `/sign/[token]` is in the `src/proxy.ts:48` public-page allowlist, SSR uses `createServiceClient` not user session, the PDF fetch goes to a Supabase signed URL on a different origin so app-domain cookies don't follow, and the pdfjs worker is served from `_next/static/media/...` (matcher-exempt). Login state was not the differentiator. Live AAA-prod verification PASS via Eric clicking the contract link from `/email` after Vercel deploy — verbatim "it worked." `npx tsc --noEmit` clean; no build verified (single-token edit, zero type or runtime risk; Vercel auto-deployed). **Customer impact:** real but narrow — only customers whose email client renders the body inside a sandboxed iframe (Gmail web, Outlook web, the in-app `/email` inbox) hit this; native mail clients (Apple Mail, Outlook desktop, mobile mail apps) don't sandbox the rendered body so most real-world signing flows would not have hit this. **All four 15h UX findings now closed.** Memorized the linkage to project memory `project_email_iframe_sandbox_popups.md` so future sandbox-tightening on `<EmailBodyFrame>` doesn't re-break signing — `allow-scripts` MUST stay omitted on the iframe itself (email bodies must not execute scripts), `allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox` is the only correct way to break the inheritance chain. Diagnosis fully controller-driven via `mcp__claude-in-chrome__*` (one `browser_batch` call combining `javascript_tool` + `read_console_messages` + `read_network_requests` was decisive); zero subagents this session. See [[2026-05-08-build-15h-followup-chrome-sign-sandbox]].

Added `window.Capacitor?.isNativePlatform?.() === true` to the OR condition. **No native plugin install required:** iPadOS 16.4+ supports Web Share with files inside WKWebView natively, plain web `navigator.share({ files })` works without `@capacitor/share`. **No new TestFlight build needed for the fix** — `capacitor.config.ts:9` sets `server.url = 'https://aaaplatform.vercel.app'` so the iPad TestFlight app is a thin WKWebView loading live Vercel content; web changes propagate on next app launch. [[build-15f]] + [[build-15g]] **Signature pad Type mode + send-body signing_link guard-rail — FULLY SHIPPED 2026-05-07.** Two tightly-coupled sub-builds that landed in a single session on top of 15d. **15f** rewrites `src/components/contracts/signature-pad-modal.tsx` (123 → 234 lines, single-file change) — bumps draw stroke `lineWidth` 2 → 3.5 + adds `lineJoin = "round"` + replaces per-pointer `lineTo + stroke` with quadratic-curve midpoint smoothing (standard `signature_pad`-library pattern, eliminates polyline kinks at the heavier weight); adds a Type tab (text input + 200px live HTML preview rendered in **Caveat** Google font via `next/font/google` mirroring `Inter` in `app/layout.tsx:2`) that on Insert renders the typed name onto an offscreen 600×200 canvas via `ctx.fillText` with auto-shrink-to-fit (60 → 28px floor at 4px steps until `measureText.width < 560`) and exports PNG via `toDataURL("image/png")` — **zero backend change** because both tabs emit through the existing `onConfirm(dataUrl: string)` contract and the server-side `stamp-pdf.ts` + `/api/sign/[token]` POST + pdf-lib stamping path is byte-identical regardless of which tab sourced the PNG; adds a shared disclaimer footer ("I understand this is a legal representation of my signature." — exact HelloSign verbatim, ESIGN-aligned, no checkbox per industry norm) with Cancel + Insert buttons (Confirm renamed Insert). Tab a11y wired with `role="tablist"` / `role="tab"` / `aria-selected` / `aria-controls`. Font-load race guarded by `await document.fonts.load("60px Caveat")` before the offscreen render + a pre-warm on modal open. Tab-switch preserves both states (typed text + drawn ink); canvas re-initializes on each return to Draw because preserving `<canvas>` state inside a `hidden` tabpanel was deemed fragile and out of scope. Sole caller `contract-signer-view.tsx:219` unchanged. Spec at `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-07-signature-pad-type-mode-design.md` (commit `669996d`); 3-task plan at `docs/superpowers/plans/2026-05-07-signature-pad-type-mode.md` (commit `fdfdcd0`); feat commit `9852ee4`. **15g** is a guard-rail surfaced during 15f end-to-end smoke when Eric replaced the default email body with the literal string `TESTINGGGGGGG` for a test send — Resend accepted dispatch (contract `6a9eaac0-1825-4297-b96d-65915c97ae38`, message_id `89306a36-e156-4d49-8a0e-01f8c61187e3`), Eric received the email, but it had no link to sign. Root cause: server-side `applyMergeFieldValues` in `src/lib/contracts/merge-fields.ts:211` is a **substitution-only** resolver — replaces existing tokens but never prepends missing ones; body lacked `{{signing_link}}` → resolver had nothing to substitute → email rendered as just the test text. Two-layer fix in commit `a1dfb06`: **server** at `src/app/api/contracts/send/route.ts` rejects HTTP 400 when the request body lacks `{{signing_link}}` (accepts either `{{double_brace}}` or the Tiptap pill form `data-field-name="signing_link"`, matching what the resolver recognizes; error copy "Email body must contain the {{signing_link}} placeholder so the recipient gets a sign-in link."); **client** at `src/components/contracts/send-contract-modal.tsx` derives `bodyHasSigningLink` using the same regex/contains check, renders an inline red warning under the body editor when the user has typed something but lacks the token, and disables the Send button while the token is missing (submit-time toast as final fallback). End-to-end verified against prod Vercel: SendContract modal correctly disabled Send when body was blanked, restoring `{{signing_link}}` re-enabled it, fresh contract sent + email arrived w/ working link, signing page opened the new tabbed modal, both Draw + Type tabs produced PNGs that were stamped onto the contract PDF, auto-shrink + tab-switch preservation + disclaimer copy all PASS. **Signing URL recovery technique discovered:** when a contract goes out with a broken email body but the row is in DB with a valid `link_token`, `SELECT link_token FROM contracts WHERE id = '<id>'` via Supabase MCP returns the JWT and constructing `https://aaaplatform.vercel.app/sign/<token>` gives a working fallback URL — used today to recover Jadon's `6a9eaac0` contract without re-sending. **Latent risk noted (deferred):** Tiptap's Link extension default `validate` may strip non-URL hrefs like `{{signing_link}}` if the editor round-trips through `editor.getHTML()` on edit; today's bug was simpler (full body replacement) so this pathway wasn't exercised, but if a user edits the body without explicitly removing the link, the post-Tiptap-stripped body could lack the token. The new guards catch this case correctly (token-less body → guard fires); for a stronger fix, configure Tiptap's Link extension with a permissive `validate` inside the SendContractModal's email-body editor so `{{signing_link}}` survives the round-trip. See [[2026-05-07-build-15f-15g-signature-pad-and-send-guardrail]].

Spec at `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-06-build-15d-contract-template-pdf-overlay-design.md` (`e9c66e9`); 30-task implementation plan at `docs/superpowers/plans/2026-05-06-build-15d-contract-template-pdf-overlay.md` (`d030c5a`). **27/30 plan tasks shipped** in a single implementation session 2026-05-06 (commits `f04ef1c` → `d3b3f3b`, 29 commits unpushed at session end). **Replaced** the existing Tiptap-based contract template editor with a PDF-upload + drag-overlay-fields builder. Authors upload a finished PDF (e.g. AAA's existing FM-7001 work-authorization contract), drop six kinds of overlay fields onto exact coordinates per page (merge field, signature, date, free-text label, customer-fillable input, checkbox); at sign-time the customer fills any inputs/checkboxes and signs in-browser, and the server stamps all values onto a copy of the PDF using `pdf-lib` and stores the stamped PDF as the signed contract artifact. **The Tiptap editor (`src/components/contracts/template-editor.tsx`, `merge-field-node.ts`, `merge-field-sidebar.tsx`) is retired in Task 25** along with the legacy tablet-signing-form + signing-form components (deleted earlier in Task 24); the 685-line HTML→PDF renderer (`src/lib/contracts/pdf.ts`) and the orphan email/regenerate routes are deferred to Task 25b (likely 15e). Schema migration `build15d_contract_pdf_overlays` applied to prod 2026-05-06: dropped `contract_templates.{content, content_html, default_signer_count}` and added `pdf_storage_path/pdf_page_count/pdf_pages/overlay_fields/signer_count/version`; new private bucket `contract-pdfs` with 4 RLS policies; existing `Contract.signed_pdf_path` reused for stamped final + `customer_inputs JSONB` for fill-time values. Stack: `react-pdf` ^10 (wraps pdfjs-dist) for in-browser rendering in editor + customer view; `pdf-lib` ^1.17 for server-side stamping. **Distinct from 67c1's `@react-pdf/renderer` stack** — that one builds PDFs from React; `pdf-lib` modifies existing PDF bytes; both libs ship together post-15d. Drag-from-palette UX (industry-standard DocuSign/PandaDoc pattern). Coords stored as PDF points top-left; `stamp-pdf.ts` translates to bottom-left for `pdf-lib` at draw time. Auto-save with 1s debounce + 409 stale-check via `version` column (reuses 67a pattern). **What shipped this session by phase:** Tasks 1–9 pre-flight + deps + worker + schema migration + bucket + types/helpers/`stamp-pdf.ts` + overlay-fields zod validator. Tasks 10–13 the 5 template API routes (POST create-empty, POST+GET PDF upload, PATCH save, POST duplicate accept overlay payload, GET preview sample-stamped PDF). Tasks 14–20 the 7 editor components: `<TemplatePdfUploadZone>`, `<PdfCanvas>` (react-pdf rendering with per-page drop layer), `<OverlayFieldChip>` (drag-to-move + corner resize), `<FieldPalette>` + `<FieldInspector>`, `<TemplatePdfEditor>` three-pane orchestrator, edit-page route swap, templates list page page-count + signer-count badges. Tasks 21–24 signing flow rewrite: `<ContractSignerView>` + extracted `<SignaturePadModal>`, `/api/sign/[token]` GET (returns `PublicSigningView` payload) + POST (stamps on all-signed via `stampPdf`), `/api/contracts/in-person` admin POST mirror, signing pages wired through `<ContractSignerView>` + new `<InPersonSigningWrapper>` for `useRouter`. **Post-review fixes (commit `8cbaab5`)** addressed two critical bugs caught by code-quality review that the implementer's self-review missed: (a) multi-signer in-person flow was redirecting to `/complete` after signer 1 (now branches on `all_signed`); (b) `"use server"` directive misapplied to a Page (removed). Same commit refactored to a shared `build-public-signing-view.ts` helper called by both the API route and the in-person page (eliminated server-side `fetch` to own origin + duplicated view-shape construction); added `<SignedRedirectWrapper>` so the email-link path refreshes after sign and shows `<SignedShell>`. **Task 26** (preview consumers): `preview-contract-modal.tsx` rewritten as iframe wrapper of `/api/settings/contract-templates/[id]/preview`; `send-contract-modal.tsx` and `sign-in-person-modal.tsx` simplified to drop legacy preview-fetch dance. Code-quality review found a permission-gate bug — preview endpoint was gated on `manage_contract_templates` but called from non-admin send modals; fix at commit `8e08060` falls back to "authenticated org member" if the manage check fails (sample-only data; matches the bar the send routes already use). **Task 27** (tsc-driven sweep) surfaced TWO production-blocking bugs in DRAFT-creation routes the plan never enumerated: `/api/contracts/in-person/start` and `/api/contracts/send` were still doing `select("content_html") + resolveMergeFields(html, jobData) + insert filled_content_html=resolved` and would have crashed at runtime against the post-15d schema. Both rewritten (commit `56bba7f`) to drop merge pre-resolution (defer to sign time) and validate `pdf_storage_path` instead of `content_html`. Empty string + sha256-of-empty placeholder passed for the still-NOT-NULL `contracts.filled_content_html` column. Two orphans deleted: `src/app/api/contracts/preview/route.ts` (legacy HTML preview, no callers) + `src/components/contracts/preview-modal.tsx` (no importers). Final `refactor(15d): hoist legacy filled_content_html placeholder to constant` (commit `d3b3f3b`) put `EMPTY_HTML` and `EMPTY_HTML_SHA256` into `src/lib/contracts/constants.ts` to dedupe the magic-hash. Plus `fix(15d): correct react-pdf v10 CSS import paths` (commit `5596e29`) which unblocked `npm run build` (react-pdf v10 dropped the `/esm` segment from `dist/Page/*.css`). **Pending / deferred:** Task 28 §11 manual test pass (Eric runs against prod Supabase Test Co — 12 tests covering upload + place fields + persist + preview + send + sign + multi-signer + replace PDF + legacy-contract read); Task 29 cleanup test artifacts; **Task 25b carved out** as a standalone follow-up build (likely 15e) — port email/handoff/reminder/regenerate-PDF logic from the orphan API routes (`/api/contracts/[id]/sign/route.ts` 475 lines, `/api/contracts/[id]/regenerate-pdf/route.ts`) into the new `/api/sign/[token]` + `/api/contracts/in-person` flow, then delete those orphans + `src/lib/contracts/pdf.ts`; five features unported (multi-signer next-signer email handoff, customer confirmation email with attached signed PDF, internal confirmation email with attached signed PDF, reminder scheduling, regenerate-signed-PDF endpoint). **Schema follow-up:** `contracts.filled_content_html` is still NOT NULL and the `create_contract_with_signers` RPC still demands `p_filled_content_html text` + `p_filled_content_hash text` — the placeholder workaround is fine for ship but a future migration could relax these to nullable now that no new contract writes meaningful HTML. **AAA's existing "Emergency Services" template still needs re-upload post-deploy** — migration dropped `content_html` so authoring data is gone; row identity preserved. - **[[build-15h-followup]] — Chrome `/sign/[token]` hang fix (email-iframe sandbox inheritance)** (2026-05-08 single focused session on Vanessa's MacBook Pro, `main` HEAD `d9f92ef` in sync with `origin/main`; one commit, one-line edit at `src/components/email-reader.tsx:62` adding `allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox` to the inbox iframe sandbox token list). Closes finding #4 — final 15h-deferred UX item. The in-app `/email` inbox rendered email body HTML inside `<iframe sandbox="allow-same-origin allow-popups">` with `<base target="_blank">` injected so every link opened a new tab; per HTML spec, popups from a sandboxed iframe inherit the parent's sandbox flag set unless `allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox` is also granted, so the new `/sign/[token]` tab inherited the missing `allow-scripts` and React/pdfjs scripts were blocked at parse time → 28× "Blocked script execution because document's frame is sandboxed and the 'allow-scripts' permission is not set" → SSR shell rendered but never hydrated → no PDF fetch ever attempted. Same console signature 15e fixed for a different cause (pdf.js fake-worker fallback iframe was sandboxed); this time the parent tab itself was sandboxed via inheritance — cause was upstream. **Diagnosis was the work; the fix was one token.** Three-context repro nailed it (incognito-paste OK, MCP-controlled tab in same Chrome profile OK with workerSrc + SW + cache state all healthy, click-from-email still hung — differentiator was the navigation path, not the URL or cache or login state). Eric's "logged in on Chrome but not on Safari?" hypothesis ruled out via proxy allowlist + service-role SSR + cross-origin PDF fetch + matcher-exempt worker. Live AAA-prod verification PASS via Eric clicking the contract link from `/email` after Vercel deploy, verbatim "it worked." Customer impact narrow — affects email clients that sandbox the rendered body (Gmail web, Outlook web, the in-app `/email` inbox); native mail clients (Apple Mail, Outlook desktop, mobile mail) don't, so most real-world signing flows would not have hit it. **All four 15h UX findings now closed.** Diagnosis fully controller-driven via `mcp__claude-in-chrome__*` (zero subagents); memorized the linkage to project memory `project_email_iframe_sandbox_popups.md` so future hardening on `<EmailBodyFrame>` doesn't re-break signing. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean. No DB migrations. No new tests. See [[2026-05-08-build-15h-followup-chrome-sign-sandbox]].

## Major shipped systems

- **Phase 1 platform** (Builds 1–10) — core jobs, customers, scheduling, photos. See [[build-1-10]], [[build-11]] (photo annotator).
- **Email** — inbox + attachments ([[build-12]], [[build-13]]); categories + body-pattern rules ([[build-27]], [[build-28]]).
- **Settings hub** (Build 14a–i) — company, appearance, statuses, auth, signatures, intake form, notifications, reports, export. See [[build-14a]]…[[build-14h-14i]].
- **Contracts** (Build 15a–c) — templates, remote signing, in-person/multi-signer/reminders. See [[build-15a]], [[build-15b]], [[build-15c]].
- **Accounting + QuickBooks** (Build 16a–d) — expenses, dashboard, QB connection, invoice/payment sync. See [[build-16a]], [[build-16b]], [[build-16c]], [[build-16d]].
- **Stripe payments** (Build 17a–c) — Connect + payment requests, public `/pay` page + emails, webhook + receipts/refunds + QB bridge. See [[build-17a]], [[build-17b]], [[build-17c]].
- **Jarvis AI assistant ecosystem** at `/jarvis` and `/api/jarvis`; knowledge base at `/settings/knowledge`. Four agents (Jarvis Core, R&D, Field Ops, Marketing) — see [[jarvis]]. Backed by **migrations 21, 23, 25a, 26b**. Marketing also has its own page at `/marketing` (Social Media + Chat tabs) — see [[build-26b]]. The Marketing **module** is the Jarvis Marketing sub-agent surfaced via a dedicated page.
- **Job UI iterations** — nav order ([[build-29]]), files section ([[build-30]]), insurance + photos redesign ([[build-31]]), soft-delete jobs + 30-day trash ([[build-66]]).
- **Multi-tenant infrastructure** — schema + backfill ([[build-18a]], migrations 42–54), RLS enforcement ([[build-18b]], migrations 55–60), workspace switcher ([[build-18c]], migrations 62/62b/63). `handle_new_user` trigger restoration follow-up: [[build-64]].
- **Capacitor iOS shell** — [[build-65a]]. Shipped to TestFlight as Nookleus. Live-bundle WebView per [[2026-04-26-capacitor-live-bundle]]; flips to bundled-static at 65e.
- **Knowledge vault** — scaffolding [[build-66a]], audit-first backfill [[build-66b]], skills [[build-66c]], per-machine Obsidian setup [[build-66d]]. All shipped 2026-04-29.
- **Estimates & Invoices Foundation** — [[build-67a]]. Estimate creation entry, full builder UI (sections + subsections + line items, dnd-kit reorder, Tiptap statements, AddItemDialog with library + custom tabs, TotalsPanel with markup/discount/tax + minimize), auto-save with retry/backoff/409 stale handling, read-only view, job-page integration. 67b adds estimate templates + invoice editor reusing the builder shell + estimate-to-invoice conversion. 67c1 adds PDF generation + Manager/Editor for presets + Export modal + retires `xactimate_code`; 67c2 will add send-via-email.
- **PDF Presets + Rendering + Export** — [[build-67c1]]. `pdf_presets` table with 8-toggle slim shape (markup/discount/tax/opening/closing/category-subtotals/code-col/notes-col) + `pdfs` private Storage bucket. `/settings/pdf-presets` Manager + Editor with default rotation. `@react-pdf/renderer`-based renderer (10 files: styles + types + html-to-pdf converter + 5 atomic components + 2 mode-specific components + 2 orchestrators + render dispatcher). POST `/api/{estimates,invoices}/[id]/pdf` routes render + upload + return signed URL. Export PDF button on builder + read-only views opens preset-picker modal → browser download. AFTER INSERT trigger on `organizations` seeds default presets for new orgs.

Today only the estimate + invoice builders match that profile; future builders following the same pattern (template builders, contract editor) should adopt the same re-baseline effect. Worth flagging next time a new builder is added.

- **Camera-preview + filesystem npm packages are in `node_modules` but not declared in `package.json`.** `b388106` added them to `ios/App/CapApp-SPM/Package.swift` directly, but `cap sync` strips them on every regeneration.
